<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозрение.html>обозре́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obozrénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозрение.html>обозре́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозрение.html>обозре́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозрение.html>обозре́ний</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обозреть.html>обозре́ть</a> (30969)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зреть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zretʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозреть.html>обозре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obozrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозревать.html>обозрева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to survey, to view, to look round</li>
<li>to review, to overview</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обои.html>обо́и</a> (7351)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обои.html>обо́и</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obói</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обои.html>обо́ев</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>wallpaper
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1963</b>,  Александр Исаевич Солженицын (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aleksandr_Solzhenitsyn" class="extiw" title="w:Matryona | s Place">Matryona's Home</a> | ”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Novy_Mir" class="extiw" title="w:Novy Mir"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>Но́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоступный.html>недосту́пны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мы́ши</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́шей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:оклеить.html>окле́ил</a> матрёнину <a href = vnd.unilang:изба.html>избу́</a> рифлёными <a href = vnd.unilang:зеленоватый.html>зеленова́тыми</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:обои.html>обо́ями</a></strong>, <a href = slojóv.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">But the mice were out of reach for the cat because someone at some time, back when life was still good, had pasted Matryona's house with ribbed greenish <b>wallpaper</b>, and not just in a layer, but in five layers.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обойма.html>обо́йма</a> (8786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обойма.html>обо́йма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obójma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обойма.html>обо́ймы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обойма.html>обо́ймы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обойма.html>обо́йм</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> charger, cartridge clip</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> range, string
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:входить.html>входи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обойма.html>обойму</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vxodítʹ v obojmu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">belong to the (preferred) set</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>це́лая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обойма.html>обо́йма</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:аргумент.html>аргуме́нтов</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">célaja <b>obójma</b> arguméntov</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">a whole series of arguments</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> iron ring
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обойма.html>обо́йма</a> шарикоподшипника</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obójma šarikopodšipnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ball race</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-йти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***обойтись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обойтись.html>обойти́сь</a> (1649)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обойти.html>обойти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obojtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обойтись.html>обойти́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obojtísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обходиться.html>обходи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cost; to come to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорогой.html>до́рого</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обойтись.html>обойдётся</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto vam dórogo <b>obojdjótsja</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It will <b>cost</b> you dearly. (literal and figurative senses)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>Во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обойтись.html>обошёлся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:визит.html>визи́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветеринарный.html>ветерина́рную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:клиника.html>кли́нику</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vo skólʹko vam <b>obošólsja</b> poslédnij vizít v veterinárnuju klíniku?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">How much did your last visit to the veterinary clinic <b>cost</b> you?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to treat, to manage (with), to do (with), to make (with); to get by with (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> + instrumental case)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>Со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обойтись.html>обошли́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плохо.html>пло́хо</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">So mnoj tam <b>obošlísʹ</b> óčenʹ plóxo.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They <b>treated</b> me very badly there.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the negative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be able to do without
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>Без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учебник.html>уче́бников</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обойтись.html>обойти́сь</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Bez učébnikov ne <b>obojtísʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">One <b>cannot do without</b> textbooks.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́г</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обойтись.html>обойти́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:водка.html>во́дки</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On i dnjá ne móg <b>obojtísʹ</b> bez vódki.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>couldn't do</b> (even) a day <b>without</b> vodka.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to turn out, to work out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обойтись.html>обошло́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vsjó <b>obošlósʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Everything <b>turned out</b> all right.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обойти.html>обойти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obojtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***оболочка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оболочка.html>оболо́чка</a> (3374)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:оболочка.html>оболо́чка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oboločka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">оболочити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oboločiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*obolčьka</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*obolka</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьka</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*obelťi</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ob-</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*velťi</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оболочка.html>оболо́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obolóčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оболочка.html>оболо́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оболочка.html>оболо́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оболочка.html>оболо́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cover, envelope, shell</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> capsule, outward form</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> membrane</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> jacket, casing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shell (<i>environment</i>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оболочечник</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oboločečnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оболочечный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oboločečnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:млеть.html>млеть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mletʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be stupefied
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обомлеть.html>обомле́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ужас.html>у́жаса</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obomlétʹ</b> ot úžasa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be stupefied/frozen/ numb with terror</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборвать.html>оборва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oborvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрывать.html>обрыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tear/pluck off/round</li>
<li>to break, to tear</li>
<li>to break off (ties)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборонять.html>обороня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oboronjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***оборот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оборот.html>оборо́т</a> (3678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обороти́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oborotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборот.html>оборо́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oborót</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборот.html>оборо́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборот.html>оборо́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборот.html>оборо́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>turn, revolution (movement about an axis)</li>
<li>rotation, turnover</li>
<li>circulation</li>
<li>turnover</li>
<li>turn of events</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оборотень.html>о́боротень</a> (12741)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборотень.html>о́боротень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óborotenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборотень.html>о́боротня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборотень.html>о́боротни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборотень.html>о́боротней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>werewolf (also werefox and any other werebeast)</li>
<li>shapeshifter, turnskin</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neologism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборотень.html>о́боротни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:погон.html>пого́нах</a></span> — <i>corrupt officers of law enforcement agencies.</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборот.html>оборо́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oborót</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
